The following reactions are available under SAID
 nn- Nucleon-Nucleon elastic
 pn- Pion-Nucleon elastic. (includes Pi-N -> Pi-Pi-N)
 pr- Pion photo production
 epr- Pion electro- production
 kn- K+N elastic
 pd- Pion-deuteron -> proton-proton
 pde- Pion-deuteron elastic
 sim- Run Physics Simulations
 demo- Run SAID demo
 show- Look at .PCT file
 cprsol - setup/run comparisons for PR/EPR reactions

 Note! 
 SAID data file assignments can be changed at any time
 by entering "GO250"
 RETURN for non-graphics
 "TDL" to set PLOT time delay
 or enter TERMINAL type (XW, TK41, or ?) ->
 New contour plotter- Enter CONP or "GO60" to view
 Note new "GO55" Chi2 summary option(alternate to "GO5")
 "GO56" Summarize fits compared to Single-Energy fits
 "GO29" to do your own resonance fit
 "GO28" get decay amplitudes(A1/2,A3/2) from GW solns
 "GO57" Compare MULTIPOLES for different solutions 6/05
 "GO58" another "Compare MULTIPOLES"
 "GO59" Print/Plot amplitudes (H, F, A) vs E, S, A, t..
 "GO7" then "Go27" to PLOT PiN amplitudes for any solution
 The experimental data file is
 PR094  Photo-prod          07/09 Arndt  10/19/12                

 CAUTION! do NOT use any solution outside its range of
 validity. Extrapolation properties are generally BAD!

 Eg(photon energy) thresholds are:  
 pion=  145. eta=   707. kaon=   912. MeV
 Kindly work ABOVE these energies to avoid nonsense.
 Enter "E" here to set up for eta photoproduction
 Enter "P" here to set up for etaprime photoproduction
 Enter "L" here to set up for k-Lambda photoproduction
 Enter "S" here to set up for k-Sigma photoproduction
 Enter "B" here to switch to "Benchmark" PR data

 program by entering a "?", or "GO1" at any terminal prompt.
 The program can be exited by entering "QT" or "GO99"
 Select a desired "task" from the following list:
 0- View PICTURES of KINEMATICS, ISPIN ...
 1- Choose another solution.
 2- Set kinematics (eg Energy/Angle) for next Print/Plot.
 3- Choose an observable for Print/Plot (after kinematics).
 4- Get Chi2 from scattering data base.
 5- Enter Print/Plot for Partial Wave amplitudes.
 6- Experimental "planning" option for new(conjectured) data.
 7- Kinematic distribution of data base Print/Plot.
 8- Two-body kinematic (Lorentz) transformations.
 9- Information specific to the reaction being studied(NN..)
 11- Print PW(or Multipole) identifiers
